[gpui](index.html)

Struct Canvas Copy item path
============================

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#23-27)

```
pub struct Canvas<T> { /* private fields */ }
```

Expand description

A canvas element, meant for accessing the low level paint API without defining a whole
custom element

Trait Implementations[§](#trait-implementations)
------------------------------------------------

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#37-89)[§](#impl-Element-for-Canvas%3CT%3E)

### impl<T: 'static> [Element](trait.Element.html "trait gpui::Element") for [Canvas](struct.Canvas.html "struct gpui::Canvas")<T>

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#38)[§](#associatedtype.RequestLayoutState)

#### type [RequestLayoutState](trait.Element.html#associatedtype.RequestLayoutState) = [Style](struct.Style.html "struct gpui::Style")

The type of state returned from [`Element::request_layout`](trait.Element.html#tymethod.request_layout "method gpui::Element::request_layout"). A mutable reference to this state is subsequently
provided to [`Element::prepaint`](trait.Element.html#tymethod.prepaint "method gpui::Element::prepaint") and [`Element::paint`](trait.Element.html#tymethod.paint "method gpui::Element::paint").

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#39)[§](#associatedtype.PrepaintState)

#### type [PrepaintState](trait.Element.html#associatedtype.PrepaintState) = [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<T>

The type of state returned from [`Element::prepaint`](trait.Element.html#tymethod.prepaint "method gpui::Element::prepaint"). A mutable reference to this state is subsequently
provided to [`Element::paint`](trait.Element.html#tymethod.paint "method gpui::Element::paint").

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#41-43)[§](#method.id)

#### fn [id](trait.Element.html#tymethod.id)(&self) -> [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<[ElementId](enum.ElementId.html "enum gpui::ElementId")>

If this element has a unique identifier, return it here. This is used to track elements across frames, and
will cause a GlobalElementId to be passed to the request\_layout, prepaint, and paint methods. [Read more](trait.Element.html#tymethod.id)

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#45-47)[§](#method.source_location)

#### fn [source\_location](trait.Element.html#tymethod.source_location)(&self) -> [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<&'static [Location](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/panic/location/struct.Location.html "struct core::panic::location::Location")<'static>>

Source location where this element was constructed, used to disambiguate elements in the
inspector and navigate to their source code.

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#49-60)[§](#method.request_layout)

#### fn [request\_layout](trait.Element.html#tymethod.request_layout)( &mut self, \_id: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<&[GlobalElementId](struct.GlobalElementId.html "struct gpui::GlobalElementId")>, \_inspector\_id: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<&[InspectorElementId](struct.InspectorElementId.html "struct gpui::InspectorElementId")>, window: &mut [Window](struct.Window.html "struct gpui::Window"), cx: &mut [App](struct.App.html "struct gpui::App"), ) -> ([LayoutId](struct.LayoutId.html "struct gpui::LayoutId"), Self::[RequestLayoutState](trait.Element.html#associatedtype.RequestLayoutState "type gpui::Element::RequestLayoutState"))

Before an element can be painted, we need to know where it’s going to be and how big it is.
Use this method to request a layout from Taffy and initialize the element’s state.

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#62-72)[§](#method.prepaint)

#### fn [prepaint](trait.Element.html#tymethod.prepaint)( &mut self, \_id: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<&[GlobalElementId](struct.GlobalElementId.html "struct gpui::GlobalElementId")>, \_inspector\_id: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<&[InspectorElementId](struct.InspectorElementId.html "struct gpui::InspectorElementId")>, bounds: [Bounds](struct.Bounds.html "struct gpui::Bounds")<[Pixels](struct.Pixels.html "struct gpui::Pixels")>, \_request\_layout: &mut [Style](struct.Style.html "struct gpui::Style"), window: &mut [Window](struct.Window.html "struct gpui::Window"), cx: &mut [App](struct.App.html "struct gpui::App"), ) -> [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<T>

After laying out an element, we need to commit its bounds to the current frame for hitbox
purposes. The state argument is the same state that was returned from [`Element::request_layout()`](trait.Element.html#tymethod.request_layout "method gpui::Element::request_layout").

[Source](../src/gpui/elements/canvas.rs.html#74-88)[§](#method.paint)

#### fn [paint](trait.Element.html#tymethod.paint)( &mut self, \_id: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<&[GlobalElementId](struct.GlobalElementId.html "struct gpui::GlobalElementId")>, \_inspector\_id: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")<&[InspectorElementId](struct.InspectorElementId.html "struct gpui::InspectorElementId")>, bounds: [Bounds](struct.Bounds.html "struct gpui::Bounds")<[Pixels](struct.Pixels.html "struct gpui::Pixels")>, style: &mut [Style](struct.Style.html "struct gpui::Style"), prepaint: &mut Self::[PrepaintState](trait.Element.html#associatedtype.PrepaintState "type gpui::Element::PrepaintState"), window: &mut [Window](struct.Window.html "struct gpui::Window"), cx: &mut [App](struct.App.html "struct gpui::App"), )

Once layout has been completed, this method will be called to paint the element to the screen.
The state argument is the same state that was returned from [`Element::request_layout()`](trait.Element.html#tymethod.request_layout "method gpui::Element::request_layout").

[Source](../src/gpui/element.rs.html#107-109)[§](#method.into_any)

Convert this element into a dynamically-typed [`AnyElement`](struct.AnyElement.html "struct gpui::AnyElement").

[Source](../src/gpui/styled.rs.html#372-379)[§](#method.bg)

[Source](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/downcast_rs/lib.rs.html#189)[§](#impl-Downcast-for-T)

### impl<T> [Downcast](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/downcast_rs/trait.Downcast.html "trait downcast_rs::Downcast") for T where T: [Any](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/any/trait.Any.html "trait core::any::Any"),

[Source](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/downcast_rs/lib.rs.html#190)[§](#method.into_any-1)

#### fn [into\_any](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/downcast_rs/trait.Downcast.html#tymethod.into_any)(self: [Box](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/boxed/struct.Box.html "struct alloc::boxed::Box")<T>) -> [Box](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/boxed/struct.Box.html "struct alloc::boxed::Box")<dyn [Any](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/any/trait.Any.html "trait core::any::Any")>

Convert `Box<dyn Trait>` (where `Trait: Downcast`) to `Box<dyn Any>`. `Box<dyn Any>` can
then be further `downcast` into `Box<ConcreteType>` where `ConcreteType` implements `Trait`.

[Source](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/downcast_rs/lib.rs.html#191)[§](#method.into_any_rc)

#### fn [into\_any\_rc](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/downcast_rs/trait.Downcast.html#tymethod.into_any_rc)(self: [Rc](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/rc/struct.Rc.html "struct alloc::rc::Rc")<T>) -> [Rc](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/rc/struct.Rc.html "struct alloc::rc::Rc")<dyn [Any](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/any/trait.Any.html "trait core::any::Any")>

Convert `Rc<Trait>` (where `Trait: Downcast`) to `Rc<Any>`. `Rc<Any>` can then be
further `downcast` into `Rc<ConcreteType>` where `ConcreteType` implements `Trait`.

[Source](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/downcast_rs/lib.rs.html#192)[§](#method.as_any)

#### fn [as\_any](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/downcast_rs/trait.Downcast.html#tymethod.as_any)(&self) -> &(dyn [Any](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/any/trait.Any.html "trait core::any::Any") + 'static)

Convert `&Trait` (where `Trait: Downcast`) to `&Any`. This is needed since Rust cannot
generate `&Any`’s vtable from `&Trait`’s.

[Source](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/downcast_rs/lib.rs.html#193)[§](#method.as_any_mut)

#### fn [as\_any\_mut](https://docs.rs/downcast-rs/1.2.1/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/downcast_rs/trait.Downcast.html#tymethod.as_any_mut)(&mut self) -> &mut (dyn [Any](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/any/trait.Any.html "trait core::any::Any") + 'static)

Convert `&mut Trait` (where `Trait: Downcast`) to `&Any`. This is needed since Rust cannot
generate `&mut Any`’s vtable from `&mut Trait`’s.

[Source](../src/gpui/element.rs.html#127)[§](#impl-FluentBuilder-for-T)

#### fn [into](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/convert/trait.Into.html#tymethod.into)(self) -> U

Calls `U::from(self)`.

That is, this conversion is whatever the implementation of
`From<T> for U` chooses to do.

if `into_left` is `true`.

otherwise. [Read more](https://docs.rs/either/1.15.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/into_either/trait.IntoEither.html#method.into_either)
